.. _doxid-_l_pfold_8h_1abe710a1182e6db69cc75329dfc9bed67:
.. _cid-vrna_probs_window_callback:
.. container:: typedef-container

    .. ref-code-block:: cpp
        :class: title-code-block

        typedef void () vrna_probs_window_callback (
	    FLT_OR_DBL *pr,
	    int pr_size,
	    int i,
	    int max,
	    unsigned int type,
	    void *data
	    )

    .. container:: brief-description

        Sliding window probability computation callback.

    .. container:: detailed-description

        Notes on Callback Functions This function will be called for each probability data set in the sliding window probability computation implementation of :ref:`vrna_probs_window() <doxid-group__local__pf__fold_1ga70ec33810fa17a9f67a7c59f156d0137>` . The argument *type* specifies the type of probability that is passed to this function.
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Parameters:
        
        .. list-table::
            :widths: 20 80
        
            *
                - pr
        
                - An array of probabilities
        
            *
                - pr_size
        
                - The length of the probability array
        
            *
                - i
        
                - The i-position (5') of the probabilities
        
            *
                - max
        
                - The (theoretical) maximum length of the probability array
        
            *
                - data
        
                - Auxiliary data
        
        
        
        .. admonition:: See also:
        
            :ref:`vrna_probs_window() <doxid-group__local__pf__fold_1ga70ec33810fa17a9f67a7c59f156d0137>` , :ref:`vrna_pfl_fold_up_cb() <doxid-group__local__pf__fold_1ga8958d91b1f1aebfb32b58805d141ccf3>` :ref:`VRNA_PROBS_WINDOW_BPP <doxid-group__local__pf__fold_1ga296217b76e76e5f7e6927e7210aa9b1f>` , :ref:`VRNA_PROBS_WINDOW_UP <doxid-group__local__pf__fold_1ga18325811c7dfc7b7d9d4ac37f4353615>` , :ref:`VRNA_PROBS_WINDOW_STACKP <doxid-group__local__pf__fold_1ga0a13fc668b02f21b225e2334e4caac08>` , :ref:`VRNA_EXT_LOOP <doxid-_l_pfold_8h_1af0bb577130090f6c856d1358804250bf>` , :ref:`VRNA_HP_LOOP <doxid-_l_pfold_8h_1a30170811c320f3a7b23ffff3b3343b91>` , :ref:`VRNA_INT_LOOP <doxid-_l_pfold_8h_1a956a237e7d956b684b7d593cb3eca665>` , :ref:`VRNA_MB_LOOP <doxid-_l_pfold_8h_1ad905b71f02b3799eb84b490435aec837>` , :ref:`VRNA_ANY_LOOP <doxid-_l_pfold_8h_1a1fef1ad234755db78ab6b695edce5080>`

.. _doxid-fold__vars_8h_1ab9b2c3a37a5516614c06d0ab54b97cda:
.. _cid-cut_point-2:
.. container:: global variables-container

    .. ref-code-block:: cpp
        :class: title-code-block

        int cut_point

    .. container:: brief-description

        Marks the position (starting from 1) of the first nucleotide of the second molecule within the concatenated sequence.

    .. container:: detailed-description

        To evaluate the energy of a duplex structure (a structure formed by two strands), concatenate the to sequences and set it to the first base of the second strand in the concatenated sequence. The default value of -1 stands for single molecule folding. The cut_point variable is also used by :ref:`vrna_file_PS_rnaplot() <doxid-plot__structure_8h_1abdc8f6548ba4a3bc3cd868ccbcfdb86a>` and :ref:`PS_dot_plot() <doxid-group__plotting__utils_1ga689a97a7e3b8a2df14728b8204d9d57b>` to mark the chain break in postscript plots.

Global Functions
----------------

.. _doxid-2_dpfold_8h_1a1aca740e2a75ab2b2951538266e53d64:
.. _cid-get_twodpfold_variables:
.. container:: function-container

    .. ref-code-block:: cpp
        :class: title-code-block

        :ref:`TwoDpfold_vars<doxid-struct_two_dpfold__vars>`* get_TwoDpfold_variables (
	    const char* seq,
	    const char* structure1,
	    char* structure2,
	    int circ
	    )

    .. container:: brief-description

        Get a datastructure containing all necessary attributes and global folding switches.

    .. container:: detailed-description

        This function prepares all necessary attributes and matrices etc which are needed for a call of :ref:`TwoDpfold() <doxid-2_dpfold_8h_1a9c71dafdc7450f4e643ef841394352fa>` . A snapshot of all current global model switches (dangles, temperature and so on) is done and stored in the returned datastructure. Additionally, all matrices that will hold the partition function values are prepared.
        
        Deprecated Use the new API that relies on :ref:`vrna_fold_compound_t <doxid-group__fold__compound_1ga1b0cef17fd40466cef5968eaeeff6166>` and the corresponding functions :ref:`vrna_fold_compound_TwoD() <doxid-group__fold__compound_1ga9d24b196753b4f9f03774f11661510f5>` , :ref:`vrna_pf_TwoD() <doxid-group__kl__neighborhood__pf_1ga0bc3427689bd09da09b8b3094a27f836>` , and :ref:`vrna_fold_compound_free() <doxid-group__fold__compound_1gadded6039d63f5d6509836e20321534ad>` instead!
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Parameters:
        
        .. list-table::
            :widths: 20 80
        
            *
                - seq
        
                - the RNA sequence in uppercase format with letters from the alphabet {AUCG}
        
            *
                - structure1
        
                - the first reference structure in dot-bracket notation
        
            *
                - structure2
        
                - the second reference structure in dot-bracket notation
        
            *
                - circ
        
                - a switch indicating if the sequence is linear (0) or circular (1)
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Returns:
        
        the datastructure containing all necessary partition function attributes

.. _doxid-2_dpfold_8h_1afe994291458ee2ac34d3eb825ef62a15:
.. _cid-destroy_twodpfold_variables:
.. container:: function-container

    .. ref-code-block:: cpp
        :class: title-code-block

        void destroy_TwoDpfold_variables (:ref:`TwoDpfold_vars<doxid-struct_two_dpfold__vars>`* vars)

    .. container:: brief-description

        Free all memory occupied by a :ref:`TwoDpfold_vars <doxid-struct_two_dpfold__vars>` datastructure.

    .. container:: detailed-description

        This function free's all memory occupied by a datastructure obtained from from get_TwoDpfold_variabless() or get_TwoDpfold_variables_from_MFE()
        
        Deprecated Use the new API that relies on :ref:`vrna_fold_compound_t <doxid-group__fold__compound_1ga1b0cef17fd40466cef5968eaeeff6166>` and the corresponding functions :ref:`vrna_fold_compound_TwoD() <doxid-group__fold__compound_1ga9d24b196753b4f9f03774f11661510f5>` , :ref:`vrna_pf_TwoD() <doxid-group__kl__neighborhood__pf_1ga0bc3427689bd09da09b8b3094a27f836>` , and :ref:`vrna_fold_compound_free() <doxid-group__fold__compound_1gadded6039d63f5d6509836e20321534ad>` instead!
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Parameters:
        
        .. list-table::
            :widths: 20 80
        
            *
                - vars
        
                - the datastructure to be free'd
        
        
        
        .. admonition:: See also:
        
            :ref:`get_TwoDpfold_variables() <doxid-2_dpfold_8h_1a1aca740e2a75ab2b2951538266e53d64>` , get_TwoDpfold_variables_from_MFE()

.. _doxid-2_dpfold_8h_1a692243dac482a1e158a8e1b7881cfda2:
.. _cid-twodpfoldlist:
.. container:: function-container

    .. ref-code-block:: cpp
        :class: title-code-block

        :ref:`vrna_sol_TwoD_pf_t<doxid-structvrna__sol___two_d__pf__t>`* TwoDpfoldList (
	    :ref:`TwoDpfold_vars<doxid-struct_two_dpfold__vars>`* vars,
	    int maxDistance1,
	    int maxDistance2
	    )

    .. container:: brief-description

        Compute the partition function for all distance classes.

    .. container:: detailed-description

        This function computes the partition functions for all distance classes according the two reference structures specified in the datastructure 'vars'. Similar to :ref:`TwoDfold() <doxid-group__kl__neighborhood__mfe_1ga9827e1deba983a95d0509d36b61fb0e2>` the arguments maxDistance1 and maxDistance2 specify the maximum distance to both reference structures. A value of '-1' in either of them makes the appropriate distance restrictionless, i.e. all basepair distancies to the reference are taken into account during computation. In case there is a restriction, the returned solution contains an entry where the attribute k=l=-1 contains the partition function for all structures exceeding the restriction. A values of :ref:`INF <doxid-energy__const_8h_1a12c2040f25d8e3a7b9e1c2024c618cb6>` in the attribute 'k' of the returned list denotes the end of the list
        
        Deprecated Use the new API that relies on :ref:`vrna_fold_compound_t <doxid-group__fold__compound_1ga1b0cef17fd40466cef5968eaeeff6166>` and the corresponding functions :ref:`vrna_fold_compound_TwoD() <doxid-group__fold__compound_1ga9d24b196753b4f9f03774f11661510f5>` , :ref:`vrna_pf_TwoD() <doxid-group__kl__neighborhood__pf_1ga0bc3427689bd09da09b8b3094a27f836>` , and :ref:`vrna_fold_compound_free() <doxid-group__fold__compound_1gadded6039d63f5d6509836e20321534ad>` instead!
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Parameters:
        
        .. list-table::
            :widths: 20 80
        
            *
                - vars
        
                - the datastructure containing all necessary folding attributes and matrices
        
            *
                - maxDistance1
        
                - the maximum basepair distance to reference1 (may be -1)
        
            *
                - maxDistance2
        
                - the maximum basepair distance to reference2 (may be -1)
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Returns:
        
        a list of partition funtions for the appropriate distance classes
        
        
        
        .. admonition:: See also:
        
            :ref:`get_TwoDpfold_variables() <doxid-2_dpfold_8h_1a1aca740e2a75ab2b2951538266e53d64>` , :ref:`destroy_TwoDpfold_variables() <doxid-2_dpfold_8h_1afe994291458ee2ac34d3eb825ef62a15>` , :ref:`vrna_sol_TwoD_pf_t <doxid-structvrna__sol___two_d__pf__t>`

.. _doxid-2_dpfold_8h_1ae251288f50dd4ae7d315af0085775f71:
.. _cid-twodpfold_pbacktrack:
.. container:: function-container

    .. ref-code-block:: cpp
        :class: title-code-block

        char* TwoDpfold_pbacktrack (
	    :ref:`TwoDpfold_vars<doxid-struct_two_dpfold__vars>`* vars,
	    int d1,
	    int d2
	    )

    .. container:: brief-description

        Sample secondary structure representatives from a set of distance classes according to their Boltzmann probability.

    .. container:: detailed-description

        If the argument 'd1' is set to '-1', the structure will be backtracked in the distance class where all structures exceeding the maximum basepair distance to either of the references reside.
        
        Deprecated Use the new API that relies on :ref:`vrna_fold_compound_t <doxid-group__fold__compound_1ga1b0cef17fd40466cef5968eaeeff6166>` and the corresponding functions :ref:`vrna_fold_compound_TwoD() <doxid-group__fold__compound_1ga9d24b196753b4f9f03774f11661510f5>` , :ref:`vrna_pf_TwoD() <doxid-group__kl__neighborhood__pf_1ga0bc3427689bd09da09b8b3094a27f836>` , :ref:`vrna_pbacktrack_TwoD() <doxid-group__kl__neighborhood__stochbt_1ga14aceef73f83bbde77bb3a0ca06c9d13>` , and :ref:`vrna_fold_compound_free() <doxid-group__fold__compound_1gadded6039d63f5d6509836e20321534ad>` instead!
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Parameters:
        
        .. list-table::
            :widths: 20 80
        
            *
                - vars
        
                - the datastructure containing all necessary folding attributes and matrices
        
            *
                - d1
        
                - the distance to reference1 (may be -1)
        
            *
                - d2
        
                - the distance to reference2
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Returns:
        
        A sampled secondary structure in dot-bracket notation
        
        
        
        .. admonition:: Pre-Condition
        
            The argument 'vars' must contain precalculated partition function matrices, i.e. a call to :ref:`TwoDpfold() <doxid-2_dpfold_8h_1a9c71dafdc7450f4e643ef841394352fa>` preceding this function is mandatory!
        
        
        
        .. admonition:: See also:
        
            :ref:`TwoDpfold() <doxid-2_dpfold_8h_1a9c71dafdc7450f4e643ef841394352fa>`

.. _doxid-2_dpfold_8h_1a13430ac6a7f90df426774f131647d2c7:
.. _cid-twodpfold_pbacktrack5:
.. container:: function-container

    .. ref-code-block:: cpp
        :class: title-code-block

        char* TwoDpfold_pbacktrack5 (
	    :ref:`TwoDpfold_vars<doxid-struct_two_dpfold__vars>`* vars,
	    int d1,
	    int d2,
	    unsigned int length
	    )

    .. container:: brief-description

        Sample secondary structure representatives with a specified length from a set of distance classes according to their Boltzmann probability.

    .. container:: detailed-description

        This function does essentially the same as :ref:`TwoDpfold_pbacktrack() <doxid-2_dpfold_8h_1ae251288f50dd4ae7d315af0085775f71>` with the only difference that partial structures, i.e. structures beginning from the 5' end with a specified length of the sequence, are backtracked
        
        Deprecated Use the new API that relies on :ref:`vrna_fold_compound_t <doxid-group__fold__compound_1ga1b0cef17fd40466cef5968eaeeff6166>` and the corresponding functions :ref:`vrna_fold_compound_TwoD() <doxid-group__fold__compound_1ga9d24b196753b4f9f03774f11661510f5>` , :ref:`vrna_pf_TwoD() <doxid-group__kl__neighborhood__pf_1ga0bc3427689bd09da09b8b3094a27f836>` , :ref:`vrna_pbacktrack5_TwoD() <doxid-group__kl__neighborhood__stochbt_1ga6504913303bc325659c365d5f59b41e0>` , and :ref:`vrna_fold_compound_free() <doxid-group__fold__compound_1gadded6039d63f5d6509836e20321534ad>` instead!
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Parameters:
        
        .. list-table::
            :widths: 20 80
        
            *
                - vars
        
                - the datastructure containing all necessary folding attributes and matrices
        
            *
                - d1
        
                - the distance to reference1 (may be -1)
        
            *
                - d2
        
                - the distance to reference2
        
            *
                - length
        
                - the length of the structure beginning from the 5' end
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Returns:
        
        A sampled secondary structure in dot-bracket notation
        
        
        
        .. note::
        
            This function does not work (since it makes no sense) for circular RNA sequences!
        
        
        
        .. admonition:: Pre-Condition
        
            The argument 'vars' must contain precalculated partition function matrices, i.e. a call to :ref:`TwoDpfold() <doxid-2_dpfold_8h_1a9c71dafdc7450f4e643ef841394352fa>` preceding this function is mandatory!
        
        
        
        .. admonition:: See also:
        
            :ref:`TwoDpfold_pbacktrack() <doxid-2_dpfold_8h_1ae251288f50dd4ae7d315af0085775f71>` , :ref:`TwoDpfold() <doxid-2_dpfold_8h_1a9c71dafdc7450f4e643ef841394352fa>`

.. _doxid-concentrations_8h_1a163159722a422ba90335a601fc34b8fb:
.. _cid-get_concentrations:
.. container:: function-container

    .. ref-code-block:: cpp
        :class: title-code-block

        :ref:`vrna_dimer_conc_t<doxid-group__pf__cofold_1gac48c2723444ecfdceafcfd525ca98322>`* get_concentrations (
	    double FEAB,
	    double FEAA,
	    double FEBB,
	    double FEA,
	    double FEB,
	    double* startconc
	    )

    .. container:: brief-description

        Given two start monomer concentrations a and b, compute the concentrations in thermodynamic equilibrium of all dimers and the monomers.

    .. container:: detailed-description

        This function takes an array 'startconc' of input concentrations with alternating entries for the initial concentrations of molecules A and B (terminated by two zeroes), then computes the resulting equilibrium concentrations from the free energies for the dimers. Dimer free energies should be the dimer-only free energies, i.e. the FcAB entries from the :ref:`vrna_dimer_pf_t <doxid-group__pf__cofold_1ga444df1587c9a2ca15b8eb25188f629c3>` struct.
        
        Deprecated { Use :ref:`vrna_pf_dimer_concentrations() <doxid-group__pf__cofold_1ga83b8d5d0f7875d6d5013b208f23e3356>` instead!}
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Parameters:
        
        .. list-table::
            :widths: 20 80
        
            *
                - FEAB
        
                - Free energy of AB dimer (FcAB entry)
        
            *
                - FEAA
        
                - Free energy of AA dimer (FcAB entry)
        
            *
                - FEBB
        
                - Free energy of BB dimer (FcAB entry)
        
            *
                - FEA
        
                - Free energy of monomer A
        
            *
                - FEB
        
                - Free energy of monomer B
        
            *
                - startconc
        
                - List of start concentrations [a0],[b0],[a1],[b1],...,[an][bn],[0],[0]
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Returns:
        
        vrna_dimer_conc_t array containing the equilibrium energies and start concentrations

	    const char* method_string,
	    char* method,
	    float* param_1,
	    float* param_2
	    )

    .. container:: brief-description

        Parse a character string and extract the encoded SHAPE reactivity conversion method and possibly the parameters for conversion into pseudo free energies.

    .. container:: detailed-description

        .. list-table::

            *
                - param_1
        
                - A pointer to the memory location where the first parameter of the corresponding method will be stored
        
            *
                - param_2
        
                - A pointer to the memory location where the second parameter of the corresponding method will be stored
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Returns:
        
        1 on successful extraction of the method, 0 on errors

.. _doxid-part__func__co_8h_1ae5c1e7331718669bdae7a86de2be6184:
.. _cid-co_pf_fold:
.. container:: function-container

    .. ref-code-block:: cpp
        :class: title-code-block

        :ref:`vrna_dimer_pf_t<doxid-group__pf__cofold_1ga444df1587c9a2ca15b8eb25188f629c3>` co_pf_fold (
	    char* sequence,
	    char* structure
	    )

    .. container:: brief-description

        Calculate partition function and base pair probabilities.

    .. container:: detailed-description

        This is the cofold partition function folding. The second molecule starts at the :ref:`cut_point <doxid-fold__vars_8h_1ab9b2c3a37a5516614c06d0ab54b97cda>` nucleotide.
        
        Deprecated {Use :ref:`vrna_pf_dimer() <doxid-group__pf__cofold_1ga4e5c7d06c302a7c59fc0d64dc142ca63>` instead!}
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Parameters:
        
        .. list-table::
            :widths: 20 80
        
            *
                - sequence
        
                - Concatenated RNA sequences
        
            *
                - structure
        
                - Will hold the structure or constraints
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Returns:
        
        vrna_dimer_pf_t structure containing a set of energies needed for concentration computations.
        
        
        
        .. note::
        
            OpenMP: Since this function relies on the global parameters :ref:`do_backtrack <doxid-group__model__details_1gad512b5dd4dbec60faccfe137bb474489>` , :ref:`dangles <doxid-group__model__details_1ga72b511ed1201f7e23ec437e468790d74>` , :ref:`temperature <doxid-group__model__details_1gab4b11c8d9c758430960896bc3fe82ead>` and :ref:`pf_scale <doxid-group__model__details_1gad3b22044065acc6dee0af68931b52cfd>` it is not threadsafe according to concurrent changes in these variables! Use :ref:`co_pf_fold_par() <doxid-part__func__co_8h_1aabfc6cb6d02b8f08ac4c92f4f5b125d9>` instead to circumvent this issue.

.. _doxid-part__func__co_8h_1aabfc6cb6d02b8f08ac4c92f4f5b125d9:
.. _cid-co_pf_fold_par:
.. container:: function-container

    .. ref-code-block:: cpp
        :class: title-code-block

        :ref:`vrna_dimer_pf_t<doxid-group__pf__cofold_1ga444df1587c9a2ca15b8eb25188f629c3>` co_pf_fold_par (
	    char* sequence,
	    char* structure,
	    :ref:`vrna_exp_param_t<doxid-group__energy__parameters_1ga01d8b92fe734df8d79a6169482c7d8d8>`* parameters,
	    int calculate_bppm,
	    int is_constrained
	    )

    .. container:: brief-description

        Calculate partition function and base pair probabilities.

    .. container:: detailed-description

        This is the cofold partition function folding. The second molecule starts at the :ref:`cut_point <doxid-fold__vars_8h_1ab9b2c3a37a5516614c06d0ab54b97cda>` nucleotide.
        
        Deprecated Use :ref:`vrna_pf_dimer() <doxid-group__pf__cofold_1ga4e5c7d06c302a7c59fc0d64dc142ca63>` instead!
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Parameters:
        
        .. list-table::
            :widths: 20 80
        
            *
                - sequence
        
                - Concatenated RNA sequences
        
            *
                - structure
        
                - Pointer to the structure constraint
        
            *
                - parameters
        
                - Data structure containing the precalculated Boltzmann factors
        
            *
                - calculate_bppm
        
                - Switch to turn Base pair probability calculations on/off (0==off)
        
            *
                - is_constrained
        
                - Switch to indicate that a structure contraint is passed via the structure argument (0==off)
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Returns:
        
        vrna_dimer_pf_t structure containing a set of energies needed for concentration computations.
        
        
        
        .. admonition:: See also:
        
            :ref:`get_boltzmann_factors() <doxid-group__energy__parameters_1gaef2b931c7e9d4ffb0a5c33df50ec2068>` , :ref:`co_pf_fold() <doxid-part__func__co_8h_1ae5c1e7331718669bdae7a86de2be6184>`

.. _doxid-part__func__co_8h_1a94c19120130e66a667a10a3c8598550c:
.. _cid-compute_probabilities:
.. container:: function-container

    .. ref-code-block:: cpp
        :class: title-code-block

        void compute_probabilities (
	    double FAB,
	    double FEA,
	    double FEB,
	    :ref:`vrna_ep_t<doxid-group__struct__utils_1gab9ac98ab55ded9fb90043b024b915aca>`* prAB,
	    :ref:`vrna_ep_t<doxid-group__struct__utils_1gab9ac98ab55ded9fb90043b024b915aca>`* prA,
	    :ref:`vrna_ep_t<doxid-group__struct__utils_1gab9ac98ab55ded9fb90043b024b915aca>`* prB,
	    int Alength
	    )

    .. container:: brief-description

        Compute Boltzmann probabilities of dimerization without homodimers.

    .. container:: detailed-description

        Given the pair probabilities and free energies (in the null model) for a dimer AB and the two constituent monomers A and B, compute the conditional pair probabilities given that a dimer AB actually forms. Null model pair probabilities are given as a list as produced by :ref:`assign_plist_from_pr() <doxid-group__pf__fold_1ga1cc05aaa9b0e7df2d3887e98321c2030>` , the dimer probabilities 'prAB' are modified in place.
        
        Deprecated { Use :ref:`vrna_pf_dimer_probs() <doxid-group__pf__cofold_1gaa1e39e73afb51fbaf4ae38f0c066c46b>` instead!}
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Parameters:
        
        .. list-table::
            :widths: 20 80
        
            *
                - FAB
        
                - free energy of dimer AB
        
            *
                - FEA
        
                - free energy of monomer A
        
            *
                - FEB
        
                - free energy of monomer B
        
            *
                - prAB
        
                - pair probabilities for dimer
        
            *
                - prA
        
                - pair probabilities monomer
        
            *
                - prB
        
                - pair probabilities monomer
        
            *
                - Alength
        
                - Length of molecule A

.. _doxid-part__func__co_8h_1ad94c0133157bed6912fe7fe866e0039e:

    .. container:: brief-description

        Get a pointer to the base pair probability array.

    .. container:: detailed-description

        Accessing the base pair probabilities for a pair (i,j) is achieved by

The base pair probability array is available through the :ref:`vrna_fold_compound_t <doxid-group__fold__compound_1ga1b0cef17fd40466cef5968eaeeff6166>` data structure, and its associated :ref:`vrna_mx_pf_t <doxid-group__dp__matrices_1ga68729ab3fed26bdd1806fa814f172fc1>` member.
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Returns:

    .. container:: brief-description

.. _doxid-part__func__co_8h_1a75465d7e8793db68a434d83df9a2e794:
.. _cid-update_co_pf_params_par:
.. container:: function-container

    .. ref-code-block:: cpp
        :class: title-code-block

        void update_co_pf_params_par (
	    int length,
	    :ref:`vrna_exp_param_t<doxid-group__energy__parameters_1ga01d8b92fe734df8d79a6169482c7d8d8>`* parameters
	    )

    .. container:: brief-description

        Recalculate energy parameters.

    .. container:: detailed-description

        This function recalculates all energy parameters given the current model settings. It's second argument can either be NULL or a data structure containing the precomputed Boltzmann factors. In the first scenario, the necessary data structure will be created automatically according to the current global model settings, i.e. this mode might not be threadsafe. However, if the provided data structure is not NULL, threadsafety for the model parameters :ref:`dangles <doxid-group__model__details_1ga72b511ed1201f7e23ec437e468790d74>` , :ref:`pf_scale <doxid-group__model__details_1gad3b22044065acc6dee0af68931b52cfd>` and :ref:`temperature <doxid-group__model__details_1gab4b11c8d9c758430960896bc3fe82ead>` is regained, since their values are taken from this data structure during subsequent calculations.
        
        Deprecated Use :ref:`vrna_exp_params_subst() <doxid-group__energy__parameters_1ga8e7ac4fab3b0cc03afbc134eaafb3525>` instead!
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Parameters:
        
        .. list-table::
            :widths: 20 80
        
            *
                - length
        
                - Length of the current RNA sequence
        
            *
                - parameters
        
                - data structure containing the precomputed Boltzmann factors

.. _doxid-plot__structure_8h_1abdc8f6548ba4a3bc3cd868ccbcfdb86a:
.. _cid-vrna_file_ps_rnaplot:
.. container:: function-container

    .. ref-code-block:: cpp
        :class: title-code-block

        int vrna_file_PS_rnaplot (
	    const char* seq,
	    const char* structure,
	    const char* file,
	    :ref:`vrna_md_t<doxid-group__model__details_1ga1f8a10e12a0a1915f2a4eff0b28ea17c>`* md_p
	    )

    .. container:: brief-description

        Produce a secondary structure graph in PostScript and write it to 'filename'.

    .. container:: detailed-description

        Note that this function has changed from previous versions and now expects the structure to be plotted in dot-bracket notation as an argument. It does not make use of the global :ref:`base_pair <doxid-fold__vars_8h_1a0244a629b5ab4f58b77590c3dfd130dc>` array anymore.
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Parameters:
        
        .. list-table::
            :widths: 20 80
        
            *
                - seq
        
                - The RNA sequence
        
            *
                - structure
        
                - The secondary structure in dot-bracket notation
        
            *
                - file
        
                - The filename of the postscript output
        
            *
                - md_p
        
                - Model parameters used to generate a commandline option string in the output (Maybe NULL)
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Returns:
        
        1 on success, 0 otherwise

.. _doxid-plot__structure_8h_1a139a31dd0ba9fc6612431f67de901c31:
.. _cid-vrna_file_ps_rnaplot_a:
.. container:: function-container

    .. ref-code-block:: cpp
        :class: title-code-block

        int vrna_file_PS_rnaplot_a (
	    const char* seq,
	    const char* structure,
	    const char* file,
	    const char* pre,
	    const char* post,
	    :ref:`vrna_md_t<doxid-group__model__details_1ga1f8a10e12a0a1915f2a4eff0b28ea17c>`* md_p
	    )

    .. container:: brief-description

        Produce a secondary structure graph in PostScript including additional annotation macros and write it to 'filename'.

    .. container:: detailed-description

        Same as :ref:`vrna_file_PS_rnaplot() <doxid-plot__structure_8h_1abdc8f6548ba4a3bc3cd868ccbcfdb86a>` but adds extra PostScript macros for various annotations (see generated PS code). The 'pre' and 'post' variables contain PostScript code that is verbatim copied in the resulting PS file just before and after the structure plot. If both arguments ('pre' and 'post') are NULL, no additional macros will be printed into the PostScript.
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Parameters:
        
        .. list-table::
            :widths: 20 80
        
            *
                - seq
        
                - The RNA sequence
        
            *
                - structure
        
                - The secondary structure in dot-bracket notation
        
            *
                - file
        
                - The filename of the postscript output
        
            *
                - pre
        
                - PostScript code to appear before the secondary structure plot
        
            *
                - post
        
                - PostScript code to appear after the secondary structure plot
        
            *
                - md_p
        
                - Model parameters used to generate a commandline option string in the output (Maybe NULL)
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Returns:
        
        1 on success, 0 otherwise

.. _doxid-profiledist_8h_1abe75e90e00a1e5dd8862944ed53dad5d:

.. container:: function-container

    .. ref-code-block:: cpp
        :class: title-code-block

        float profile_edit_distance (
	    const float* T1,
	    const float* T2
	    )

    .. container:: brief-description

        Align the 2 probability profiles T1, T2
        
        .

    .. container:: detailed-description

        This is like a Needleman-Wunsch alignment, we should really use affine gap-costs ala Gotoh

.. _doxid-profiledist_8h_1a3dff26e707a2a2e65a0f759caabde6e7:
.. _cid-make_bp_profile_bppm:
.. container:: function-container

    .. ref-code-block:: cpp
        :class: title-code-block

        float* Make_bp_profile_bppm (
	    :ref:`FLT_OR_DBL<doxid-group__data__structures_1ga31125aeace516926bf7f251f759b6126>`* bppm,
	    int length
	    )

    .. container:: brief-description

        condense pair probability matrix into a vector containing probabilities for unpaired, upstream paired and downstream paired.

    .. container:: detailed-description

        This resulting probability profile is used as input for profile_edit_distance
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Parameters:
        
        .. list-table::
            :widths: 20 80
        
            *
                - bppm
        
                - A pointer to the base pair probability matrix
        
            *
                - length
        
                - The length of the sequence
        
        
        
        .. rubric:: Returns:
        
        The bp profile
